  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_ef5b9739-2cbc-4bb4-8840-63a5d949c457'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText13277890037957021350" style="display:none">"Not since Nora Roberts has anyone been able to write a big family romance series with every book as good as the last. Bella Andre never disappoints." Revolving Bookcase Reviews<br /><br />Millions of readers around the world have fallen in love with Bella Andre’s New York Times and USA Today bestselling contemporary romances about the Sullivans!<br /><br />Can two people who have both sworn off love find forever in each other's arms? The last thing Zach Sullivan wants is to take care of his brother's new puppy for two weeks. Until he meets the dog trainer, that is. Heather is bright, beautiful, and he can't stop thinking about her. Unfortunately, she just might be the only woman on earth who wants nothing to do with him.<br /><br />Heather Linsey can't believe she's stuck working with one of the city's top dogs, auto-shop tycoon Zach Sullivan. Especially when his focus is clear from the start--not only to learn how to deal with his temporary puppy...but also to make Heather his. Having sworn off love at seventeen when she realized it was nothing more than a pack of lies, she has stuck to her vow never to fall for a charming man.<br /><br />But as Heather's determination to push Zach away only fuels his determination to get closer--and the sensual and emotional connection between them grows more and more undeniable--will the biggest Sullivan bad boy of all tempt her into believing in love again?<br /><br />IF YOU WERE MINE is part of Bella Andre's #1 bestselling series about The Sullivans. While it can easily be read as a stand-alone story, you'll likely enjoy reading the other books, too.<br /><br />THE SULLIVANS: <br />The Look of Love <br />From This Moment On <br />Can't Help Falling In Love <br />I Only Have Eyes For You <br />If You Were Mine <br />Let Me Be The One <br />Come A Little Bit Closer <br />Always On My Mind <br />Kissing Under The Mistletoe <br />One Perfect Night<br />The Way You Look Tonight<br />It Must Be Your Love<br />Just To Be With You<br />I Love How You Love Me<br />All I Ever Need Is You<br />Now That I've Found You<br />Since I Fell For You<br /><br />THE MAVERICK BILLIONAIRES:<br />Breathless In Love<br />Reckless In Love<br />Fearless In Love<br /><br />THE MORRISONS:<br />Kiss Me Like This<br />Tempt Me Like This<br />Love Me Like This<br /><br /><br />REVIEWS:<br />“Each book is so remarkable and you really come to love the characters. This series is incredible. It's one of my favorites. If you haven't started them yet, you are missing out!" ~ Guilty Pleasures Reviews<br /><br /><br />"I am in love with the Sullivans.           $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('edition_17738212').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('edition_17738212').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });

        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-contemporary-romance">genre-contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers">keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer335747070" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5176014026669217945"><b> Posted on<a href='http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.ca/2012/05/review-if-you-were-mine-by-bella-andre.html' rel='nofollow noopener'> Under the Covers</a></b><br/><br/> <b>Dear Mrs. Andre,<br/><br/> You really must stop this. I can’t believe I am saying this but, you need to stop making your heroes so damn sexy! I don’t have enough space in my hottie harem and I have always said I would never do brothers, let alone four of them (plus Jake!) But when you make your heroes as irresistible as Zach, I fall prey to your every whim and now I am eating my words. What’s one more Sullivan in my harem, right? Hell, I might as well claim them all!<br/><br/> Love, Ann </b></span>
  <span id="freeText5176014026669217945" style="display:none"><b> Posted on<a href="http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.ca/2012/05/review-if-you-were-mine-by-bella-andre.html" rel="nofollow noopener"> Under the Covers</a></b><br /><br /> <b>Dear Mrs. Andre,<br /><br /> You really must stop this. I can’t believe I am saying this but, you need to stop making your heroes so damn sexy! I don’t have enough space in my hottie harem and I have always said I would never do brothers, let alone four of them (plus Jake!) But when you make your heroes as irresistible as Zach, I fall prey to your every whim and now I am eating my words. What’s one more Sullivan in my harem, right? Hell, I might as well claim them all!<br /><br /> Love, Ann </b><br /><br /><br />IF YOU WERE MINE takes readers back into the lives of the family we have come to love. This time we follow Zach Sullivan, the mogul mechanic, sweet-talker and all around panty-melter. As the hands-down most hottest of the Sullivan brothers, Zach is used to getting attention from the ladies. He has it all – the money, the good looks and the fancy cars. But when Heather Lindsey walks into his life, Zach finds the one thing his perfect life is missing...<br /><br />Zach is on babysitting duty for his brother-in-law’s puppy. The small and unsuspecting Yorkie is the devil in disguise and unfortunately for Zach, Cuddles is stuck with him for two weeks. So while Zach tries his best to keep Cuddles out of his garage and his way, Heather drops in to teach the big boss how to handle a puppy.<br /><br />When Zach meets the new dog trainer Heather, he is taken aback by her beauty and knows that soon, he will have her eating out of the palm of his hand. Unfortunately, Heather is the one is doing the talk-to-the-hand gesture because she knows all about Zach Sullivan and his reputation with the ladies. And to protect her heart, Heather knows it’s best to stay away. Despite the barriers she has walled around her, Zach’s relentless determination has her grasping for control because day by day, Heather learns more about Zach and fears that she is falling for him.<br /><br />Andre has another winner on her hands! I wasn’t sure how she would be able to top the last two books (both of which were my favorites of the series), but she has. Zach Sullivan definitely has what it takes to be crowned the hottest Sullivan. His possessiveness, determination and unexpected vulnerability made me love him completely. But it was his charm that really made me fall in love with Zach. Unlike the other Sullivans, he is great at the witty banter and I guess it helps whenever he does that slow smile that makes the ladies burn.<br /><br />Zach was easy to love, but Heather also had a lot of emotional depth to her. We learn of her past and the not so bright moments of that time in her life. Her parents are together, but unhappy and that reflects back on how Heather sees men and relationships. The question is, whether or not she will allow Zach to help her overcome those fears and feel safe with him.<br /><br />Their love develops slowly, but it is satisfying because at the end of the book, you feel as if both of them have crossed oceans to get where they are supposed to be. I loved every moment of this book and only wished there was more to devour.<br /><br />Andre is a master storyteller, weaving together the lives of two characters who simple don’t know the meaning of love...until they meet each other. Loved it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="5176014026669217945" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <blockquote>"The thing was, he wanted Heather bad enough that he was willing to break a few rules for her. Not the big one, of course. He wasn't going to fall in love with her or anything." </blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>Another great installment to the Sullivan's series. Each book that I've read by this author has been consistently good. Although I must say that the spice level has gone down noticeable within the last couple of books. And that was one thing that I liked about Bella Andre...she wrote a great romance story but include</span>
  <span id="freeText14740716662092413320" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>"The thing was, he wanted Heather bad enough that he was willing to break a few rules for her. Not the big one, of course. He wasn't going to fall in love with her or anything." </blockquote>
</b><br><br>Another great installment to the Sullivan's series. Each book that I've read by this author has been consistently good. Although I must say that the spice level has gone down noticeable within the last couple of books. And that was one thing that I liked about Bella Andre...she wrote a great romance story but included hot sex. This was still sexy, but I honestly felt the sexy was a bit lackluster...and that may be entirely due to my expectations being different.<br><br>Aside from that little grump, I quite enjoyed the rest of the story. Zach is the hottest of the hot Sullivan siblings...he owns a chain of autobody shops and is doing quite well for himself. Although the only part of his lifestyle that really entered into the story was how he filled in for the driver of a racing car that he sponsors. Totally unrealistic, but hey...it worked. <br><br>Heather becomes involved with Ryan after another Sullivan sibling dumps a new puppy in his lap for a two week long dog sitting session. Of course, Zach has no idea what to do with the rambunctious little girl...aptly named "Cuddles". So Heather, the owner of a dog training school, steps in to try to tame the beast...owner and doggie alike. Sparks fly, but Heather is adamant that she will never enter into a relationship in which she can be hurt. Girl has Daddy issues, in a major way.<br><br>Once again, this book is full to the brim with romance tropes, and yet Andre makes is feel fresh and new. I'm an animal lover, so the way that Zach's sweet little pup melts his heart...well...it' melted my heart as well. <br>Zach's ward Cuddles, a Yorkshire Terrier:<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414227i/816458._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Heather's Atlas, a Great Dane<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414227i/816459._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1339033825149829766">17/8 - This book has a few flaws, but reading it makes my heart feel all warm and smushy. There's a ton of doggy love which had me running to snuggle with my doggy and plenty of smoking hot sex scenes between Zach and Heather, in fact the second half of the book was practically one long sex scene with a few breaks in between to feed and toilet the dogs.   <span id="freeText1339033825149829766" style="display:none">17/8 - This book has a few flaws, but reading it makes my heart feel all warm and smushy. There's a ton of doggy love which had me running to snuggle with my doggy and plenty of smoking hot sex scenes between Zach and Heather, in fact the second half of the book was practically one long sex scene with a few breaks in between to feed and toilet the dogs. Zach and Heather were fully fleshed-out characters, but other than the rest of the Sullivan gang, there were no secondary characters that weren't simple walk on/extra parts. I suppose you could call the dogs, Cuddles and Atlas, secondary characters, they certainly had more distinct personalities than people like Tina (Heather's assistant) or Heather's parents. I love it when it's the woman who's more reluctant to admit her feelings than the man - Zach said the magic three words first - I like the idea of a role reversal and for the guy to become the soft and slightly soppy one in the relationship (at least temporarily). Will definitely keep picking these up when I see them at the library.</span>

<div id="review_337442819" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/337442819" />
    <a title="Guilty Pleasures Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4391611-guilty-pleasures-book-reviews"><img alt="Guilty Pleasures Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1490590272p2/4391611.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/337442819?book_show_action=true">May 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Guilty Pleasures Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Guilty Pleasures Book Reviews" href="/user/show/4391611-guilty-pleasures-book-reviews">Guilty Pleasures Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4391611-guilty-pleasures-book-reviews?shelf=guiltypleasures-kittyangel">guiltypleasures-kittyangel</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer337442819" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17054877138001709012">Kitty's review posted on <a href='http://www.guiltypleasuresbookreviews.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Guilty Pleasures</a><br/><br/>Oh. My. God. How could you not love Bella Andre and the Sullivan Brothers? What a fantastic book “If You Were Mine” is. Ms. Andre again wrote another erotic, witty, humorous, loving, oh-so-sexy book about one hot “mechanic” and a beautiful dog trainer. And, how she brought them together – yes, you could see it happening in real life which is what I love about Bella Andre's books. There is nothing “out-there”; it could be a true story about how two people </span>
  <span id="freeText17054877138001709012" style="display:none">Kitty's review posted on <a href="http://www.guiltypleasuresbookreviews.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Guilty Pleasures</a><br /><br />Oh. My. God. How could you not love Bella Andre and the Sullivan Brothers? What a fantastic book “If You Were Mine” is. Ms. Andre again wrote another erotic, witty, humorous, loving, oh-so-sexy book about one hot “mechanic” and a beautiful dog trainer. And, how she brought them together – yes, you could see it happening in real life which is what I love about Bella Andre's books. There is nothing “out-there”; it could be a true story about how two people met and fell in love.*sigh* And, I think I loved the love story about Cuddles and Atlas just as much as Zach and Heather!<br /><br />Heather is a dog trainer who is sent to Zach to help him train Cuddles who he was conned into watching while Gabe, Megan and Summer go on vacation for a few weeks. Zach, being the softy that he is, just couldn't say no. But, we all know how Zach feels about woman and a “happily ever after” for himself – it's okay for his brothers but he will never give in to love. Heather doesn't believe in love either. After her father's deceit throughout her life, she doesn't trust love at all. So, friends-with-benefits it is. Or is it? They both have their secrets and their haunts from the past. It is going to take a lot for them to open up to one another. It is going to take a lot for them to see the love right in front of their eyes. With the help of family and 2 furry friends, they will not only finally believe in love but believe in the love that they have found for each other.<br /><br />As I said in the beginning, this was just a great book. I had such contradicting feelings in the beginning of “If You Were Mine”. I cried for both Heather and Zach and what they were feeling about themselves but then I was hopeful that they would be able to bring out the best of each other. I laughed with Cuddles and Atlas and was thoroughly pissed off at Heather's parents. Then, as the book went on, I just smiled and then smiled some more. The “seduction” scene in the book is unbelievable. It is so realistic and descriptive that you can feel Zach's hands on Heather, you loose your breath when she looses her's. You feel the love he is pouring into his love-making with Heather and you feel Heather falling more and more in love with Zach. There is no way to describe this scene other than wildly erotic and hot; not so much in the act itself, but in the build-up and seduction of Heather. WOW. The banter between Zach and Heather, the “mutt” and “full ball”, and all of his siblings is wonderful. Everyone is back, of course. Naughty (Lori) is still scheming (I can't wait to see how she falls) and Nice (Sophie) and Jake are still all starry-eyed. (Zach is still mad at Jake for getting Nice pregnant) Ryan and Smith just love busting on Zach and flirting with Heather now that he is falling; Chase and Chloe have their shining moment (no spoiler) and Marcus and Nicola make an appearance as well. But, there is a wonderful scene in the book between Zach and his mother Mary that had me in tears. Such a moving and poignant point in the book. Thank God for Mom's and how they know just what to say and when.<br /><br />So, the only way that I see to end this review is to thank Bella Andre for bringing us the Sullivan's; for giving us true-to-life love stories; for allowing us to become a part of the Sullivan Family, if only for a few hours while we are reading her books. If you asked me to pick just one of the Sullivan Series that would be my favorite, I would have to laugh at you. There is no way to choose. Each story is wonderfully written and flows into the next book seamlessly. Ryan – you're next – the baseball world better look out because I think Ryan and Vicki's story is going to be explosive!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17054877138001709012" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_373323166" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/373323166" />
    <a title="Jenny E" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4620170-jenny-e"><img alt="Jenny E" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1338960493p2/4620170.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

  <span id="freeText3641817480675707891" style="display:none">These books are just like chocolate... totally addicting and full of sugar! Sometimes they have the tendency to get sticky sweet, but I can't stop with this series...I really have enjoyed it. This has been the best of the series so far, which surprises me because Zach had really not piqued my interest at all in prior books. I am *DYING* for Smith's book already! <br /><br />This could have been a five-star read, I enjoyed it that much, but two things annoy me about these books. First, the kids act and talk WAY older than their age! And the biggest pet peeve is that these people are falling maddly, passionately, soul-shattering-ly (is that a word?!LOL!) in love in like a week!! Plus, I hate the condom thing every.single.sex.scene... there is no STD in Romance Fantasyland!! <br /><br />I REALLY enjoyed this book despite huge romance genre cliches... like I said, I'm addict to chocolate!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17956308924542660249">Okay, let me just summarize my feeling...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413862ra/815373.gif' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311519ra/688537.gif' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413862ra/815374.gif' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413862ra/815375.gif' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Yup, this seems about right...   <span id="freeText17956308924542660249" style="display:none">Okay, let me just summarize my feeling...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413862ra/815373.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311519ra/688537.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413862ra/815374.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413862ra/815375.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yup, this seems about right... Wow, the series has been amazing, but I think this one, along with the love story of Gabe and Megan have been the best so far!<br><br>First of all, let me just say how happy I am that the book included dogs, and not just any dogs, but two of the loveliest, friendliest and cutest dogs ever! Atlas and Cudles (yeah, way to go for a name) claimed my heart from the very beginning!<br><br>And the love story. Well, it was pretty awesome! All this love/hate, the uncertainties, the hurt, the fear made the story true, personal and made me so damn emotional that i clung to every word!<br><br>It has been an amazing experience yet again!<br><br> **********************<br><br><b>“Where the hell is that damned puppy!”<br>“You’d better get your furry little butt back here!”<br> - Jach<br><br>There were half a dozen girls in bikinis waiting in Zach’s garage, but the woman laughing with his dog in her arms, wearing a sweaty, long-sleeved T-shirt and muddy shorts, with a messy braid trailing down her back, put them all to shame. He couldn’t think of a time he’d ever seen eyes that color, brown with so many flecks of gold that he couldn’t look away. And, Jesus, that mouth of hers, rosy and full, made a man want to do crazy things...like grab the puppy and kiss it all over its drooly, disgusting little face for bringing Heather here today.<br> - Jach<br><br>“I’ve never made love to anyone before,” she whispered, overwhelmed by what she was feeling,<br>how strong, how unstoppable her emotions were.<br>He leaned closer and his mouth hovered over hers. But instead of kissing her, he whispered across<br>her lips, “Yes, you have. Every time we’ve touched, you’ve let me love you.” <br>His voice was even deeper than normal, and raw with emotion. <br>“And you’ve loved me right back.”<br> - Heather and Jach<br><br>“That’s why we should stop seeing each other—before either of us gets any deeper.” (Heather)<br>“Too late.” His eyes flashed with surprise and he stared at her in the same stunned disbelief that<br>she’d just experienced moments before. “Holy hell, I think I’m already in love with you.”<br> - Jach<br><br>“You taught me to trust. To have faith and hope. How to laugh again.” She ran the pad of her thumb<br>over his bottom lip. “And when I’m safe and warm in your arms, just like this, I know the true meaning of peace.”<br> - Heather<br><br>“You can’t change your mind about love when you don’t even believe in it, remember?”<br>“I never said I didn’t believe in love,” he clarified. “I just said I wasn’t looking for it. But I didn’t know you were coming into my life. I couldn’t have known.” He looked into eyes that were so beautiful, whether lit with laughter or hazy with passion. “I meant it when I said you were mine. From the first moment I set eyes on you, I knew it. You knew it, too, Heather. That the first time we met, the first time we touched, the first time we kissed, I was yours.”<br> - Jach<br><br>“This isn’t even about me,” she snapped back. “You just want me because I’m a challenge.”<br>“Wrong,” he shot back. “I want you because I want you. From the first second I saw you, I’ve<br>wanted you, Heather.”<br> - Jach<br><br></b>and of course:<br><b>Using the dogs to keep her close to him wasn’t playing fair.<br>Then again, when had a Sullivan ever played by the rules?</b><br><br> **********************<br><br>YES! I WANT THE NEXT BOOK! GIMME GIMME GIMME!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/511982.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3569773-paige?shelf=multiple-copies">multiple-copies</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer448832672" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6903033069024703053">In IF YOU WERE MINE, Zach Sullivan faces his greatest fear. Leaving behind his family suddenly like is father, Jack Sullivan. We learn just how the death of his father has influence Zach to live his life in the fast lane through his auto shops, women, never getting close to said women and his racing. <br/><br/>When Gabe sticks him with babysitting Summer’s new puppy Cuddles while they are on their trip, Zach is in for a surprise at just how energetic and wild the little puppy can be. <br/><br/>Luckily one of his cl</span>
  <span id="freeText6903033069024703053" style="display:none">In IF YOU WERE MINE, Zach Sullivan faces his greatest fear. Leaving behind his family suddenly like is father, Jack Sullivan. We learn just how the death of his father has influence Zach to live his life in the fast lane through his auto shops, women, never getting close to said women and his racing. <br /><br />When Gabe sticks him with babysitting Summer’s new puppy Cuddles while they are on their trip, Zach is in for a surprise at just how energetic and wild the little puppy can be. <br /><br />Luckily one of his clients sends the best dog trainer around his way. Unfortunately, they meet while he’s yelling for the lost Cuddles and get off to the wrong foot. <br /><br />Animals have been Heather Linsey’s escape since her teen cutting years and finding her impromptu client yelling for the scared puppy she finds in the bush doesn’t sit well. Despite her own dog, Atlas’, unusual good response to him, Heather refuses to let down her guard. <br /><br />Talking his way into getting training lessons keeps Heather in Zach’s reach and boy does he want her from the start. Through emergency clean ups and park trainings, Zach and Heather bond well over the dogs as well as Cuddles and Atlas who become best friends. <br /><br />Unfortunately, Zach’s playful ways and easy confidence only reinforces the hard lesson she learned from her parents’ fake marriage and she keeps her heart closed off to him. <br /><br />Until the animal shelter auction that is, when Zach make a big donation. Although she finally gives in to the attraction, they set rules for their relationship to be purely physical as both aren’t’ looking for love. <br /><br />Over the course of the two weeks, Heather learns just how wrong their first meeting and her first impression of him was. His attentiveness, love for his family (whom welcomes baby Emma), and his style breaks down the walls to her heart. <br /><br />The boastful Lori is all smiles over her victory when Zach admits his love for Heather, despite their agreement to keep it physical. <br /><br />Zach never thought he’d see the day, and still fear his time with her would be cut short, but he can’t stop denying how well she fit into his family. <br /><br />It’s when his race ends in flames that the realization of an early end sends him blocking himself off from others, including her. Giving back Cuddles, whom Summer got for him, Zach manages to lock everyone out. <br /><br />A week by themselves only reinforces their feelings as well as their sad furry friends. It’s only when his mom opens up about his father, stating even a short time with him was better than nothing, that Zach realizes he shouldn’t have pushed her away. With his mother’s engagement ring in hand, he’s off to fix things. <br /><br />Heather has the same epiphany as she realizes Zach fought for her from the beginning, yet she didn’t’ return the favor after his crash. <br /><br />Both sorry, Zach and Heather (along with Cuddles and Atlas) can spend whatever time they have left as a family, which is hopefully a long and fulfilling life. <br /><br />I’m not sure what was lacking in this for me, but it just didn’t keep me totally interested. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6903033069024703053" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_332294446" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/332294446" />
    <a title="Morgan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5637577-morgan"><img alt="Morgan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1373569756p2/5637577.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/332294446?book_show_action=true">May 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Morgan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Morgan" href="/user/show/5637577-morgan">Morgan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5637577-morgan?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer332294446" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1586799281160944197"><a href='http://www.readingeatinganddreaming.blogspot.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>CLICK HERE TO READ MORE REVIEWS AT READING, EATING AND DREAMING I WAS BLAIR WALDORF</a><br/><br/>THE FAMILY:<br/>I am in love with the Sullivans. The Sullivans are a large, one-of-a-kind family that’s made up of 8 magnificent and unique siblings.<br/><br/>Chase – Photographer (The Look of Love)<br/>Marcus – Winery (From This Moment On)<br/>Gabe – Firefighter (Can’t Help Falling in Love)<br/>Sophie (Nice) – Librarian (I Only Have Eyes For You)<br/>Zach – Auto Shop Chain (If You Were Mine)<br/>Ryan – Professional Baseball Player (TBA)<br/>Smith – Actor (T</span>
  <span id="freeText1586799281160944197" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.readingeatinganddreaming.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">CLICK HERE TO READ MORE REVIEWS AT READING, EATING AND DREAMING I WAS BLAIR WALDORF</a><br /><br />THE FAMILY:<br />I am in love with the Sullivans. The Sullivans are a large, one-of-a-kind family that’s made up of 8 magnificent and unique siblings.<br /><br />Chase – Photographer (The Look of Love)<br />Marcus – Winery (From This Moment On)<br />Gabe – Firefighter (Can’t Help Falling in Love)<br />Sophie (Nice) – Librarian (I Only Have Eyes For You)<br />Zach – Auto Shop Chain (If You Were Mine)<br />Ryan – Professional Baseball Player (TBA)<br />Smith – Actor (TBA)<br />Lori (Naughty) – Choreographer (TBA)<br /><br />THE SERIES:<br />If you are looking for something SWEET and SEXY then The Sullivans companion series by Bella Andre is absolutely perfect for you. Each novel in the companion series is unique, just like the siblings. However, there is one thing that all of the novels have in common: THEY ARE ALL AMAZING!<br /><br />I’m obsessed with this series. As soon as a new novel is released, I drop everything else so I can get my Sullivan fix.<br /><br />IF YOU WERE MINE:<br />If You Were Mine was another wonderful additional this series. I really enjoyed Zach and Heather's story. It was a sweet and sexy story with emotional undertones. I really enjoyed watching Zach and Heather try to resist falling in love.<br /><br />Zach's father died when he was a young boy leaving his mother all alone to raise eight children. Zach has always been told that he is exactly like his father, and he is convinced that he is going to die young. He doesn't want to leave a wife and children behind so he lives his life in the fast lane and doesn't form emotional attachments. One-night stands are fine but love isn't in the cards for Zach.<br /><br />Heather doesn't believe in love. Her parent's marriage looks like the perfect marriage from the outside, but Heather discovered the truth about her parent's marriage a long time ago. Her father is a cheater, and her mother is a spineless woman who looks the other way. Heather decides that if that is love, then she wants no part in it.<br /><br />Overall, If You Were Mine was a fabulous story. I only have one minor critique, and bare with me because I am going to keep things vague to avoid any spoilers. Bella Andre brought up a serious issue in this novel, but in my opinion, she could have delved a little deeper into this issue. She "talked" about it, but she never really "explored" it. I would connected with Heather better if I would have been able to understand her past struggles better. Did this keep me from loving the story? No. I still strongly recommend this story and this series.<br /><br />I gave If You Were Mine by Bella Andre 4 STARS. If you haven't been introduced to the Sullivans yet, then I recommend that you fix that immediately, starting with the first novel in the companion series, The Look of Love. <br /><br />-XOXO<br /><br /><a href="http://www.readingeatinganddreaming.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">READING, EATING AND DREAMING</a></span>

  <span id="freeText12828155241284699652" style="display:none">This book started out fun and really enjoyable. I really liked the characters and I enjoy the Sullivan family as a whole. But honestly it's as though this author cannot write a book without a big, stupid separation. Not even a good one. As as the story goes, you're just waiting for it. <div id="review_336731745" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/336731745" />
    <a title="Tori Macallister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7582222-tori-macallister"><img alt="Tori Macallister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1330993011p2/7582222.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/336731745?book_show_action=true">May 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tori Macallister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tori Macallister" href="/user/show/7582222-tori-macallister">Tori Macallister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7582222-tori-macallister?shelf=the-latest">the-latest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7582222-tori-macallister?shelf=in-kindle">in-kindle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer336731745" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1222984426188405845">Originally published at <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.torimacallister.com'>http://www.torimacallister.com</a> on May 26, 2012<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380378886i/734756.jpg' alt='' width='233' height='350' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <a href='http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00822SVHM/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_il_tl?ie=UTF8&tag=wwwbellaandre-20&linkCode=as2&camp=1789&creative=9325&creativeASIN=B00822SVHM' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'></a><br/><br/>My mother and I were chatting yesterday about our latest reads - actually having yet another "how does she do it?" discussion about <a title='Nora Roberts' href='http://www.noraroberts.com/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Nora Roberts</a> since we had both read and loved her latest, <em>The Witness</em> - when I hopped online to look at what the kindle edition would cost since I thought I'd be rereading it. That's when I gasped and clutched my arm as if I were having a heart attack.<br/><br/>"Jesus, what's wrong?" my mother asked, clear</span>
  <span id="freeText1222984426188405845" style="display:none">Originally published at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.torimacallister.com">http://www.torimacallister.com</a> on May 26, 2012<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380378886i/734756.jpg" alt="" width="233" height="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00822SVHM/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_il_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;tag=wwwbellaandre-20&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;creativeASIN=B00822SVHM" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br>My mother and I were chatting yesterday about our latest reads - actually having yet another "how does she do it?" discussion about <a title="Nora Roberts" href="http://www.noraroberts.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Nora Roberts</a> since we had both read and loved her latest, <em>The Witness</em> - when I hopped online to look at what the kindle edition would cost since I thought I'd be rereading it. That's when I gasped and clutched my arm as if I were having a heart attack.<br><br>"Jesus, what's wrong?" my mother asked, clearly alarmed at my <a title="Sarah Bernhardt" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sarah_Bernhardt" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Sarah Bernhardt</a> response to looking at Amazon.com.<br><br>I pointed a finger at my MacBook screen. "Did you know that Bella Andre's latest Sullivan book came out - YESTERDAY?!"<br><br>Cue both of us grabbing our iPads and ordering it, right then and there. My mother made some excuse to leave about two minutes later claiming she was "tired from gardening." Uh-huh.<br><br>I was kicking myself that I had promised to attend a baseball playoff game, but sucked it up and made the trip (and actually had a great time). But baseball made me think of Ryan Sullivan (the Sullivan brother who is a major league baseball player), which made me think of Zach Sullivan, who we finally get to see fall, and fall <em>hard</em>, in Bella Andre's latest installment of the Sullivan family series, <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00822SVHM/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_il_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;tag=wwwbellaandre-20&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;creativeASIN=B00822SVHM" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <em>If You Were Mine</em>
</a>.<br><br>Now I haven't been shy in my deep admiration and love for all things Bella Andre. Not long ago, <a href="http://torimacallister.wordpress.com/2012/03/13/series-review-the-sullivan-series-by-bella-andre/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">I wrote a blog post on the first four books of the series, claiming that this series is one of the best values on the romance market</a> and I stand by that statement today. When so many authors, pressured to produce multiple books per year, struggle with maintaining a consistent quality, Bella Andre channels her own inner Nora Roberts and gives us another heart-stoppingly amazing addition to this series, which is claiming the spot of favorite contemporary romance series for me.<br><br>Zach Sullivan loves working with cars and enjoys the benefits of having built his love into a chain of successful automotive stations, but he enjoys fast women as much as fast cars, sporting a serious "no commitment" policy with the opposite sex. When his firefighter brother Gabe drops off the puppy of his soon-to-be stepdaughter for Zach to dogsit, Zach figures a couple pounds of puppy can't be too much for him handle. But it is. As he finds his life turned upside down by a Yorki named Cuddles, a friend sends him the best dog trainer in the San Francisco area, Heather Linsey.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380378886i/734757.jpg" alt="" width="244" height="263" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>And that "no commitment" policy gets reevaluated. Heather is far from impressed with Zach's yelling at the puppy but she quickly realizes that she's the one who might be over her head. Zach is even more good looking than his movie star brother, Smith, and his sense of humor has her more worried than his chiseled features or killer body. Heather is fine with a no commitment physical relationship, but someone who makes her laugh could find their way into her heart. The fact her faithful <a title="Great Dane" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Dane" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Great Dane</a>, Atlas, has a new best friend in Zach's puppy charge is simply another red flag on the whole situation, one that has Heather saying, "No" firmly and repeatedly to Zach's advances.<br><br>Zach hasn't really heard "no" from women before and hearing it from Heather makes him realize that they time they spend together not having sex is actually more amazing than the time he has spent having sex with other women. He knows this is dangerous, but can't stop himself from putting his heart on the line for her.<br><br>But Zach and Heather both have their own brand of damage. Heather had a terrible childhood with the discovery that her doting father, who she thought loved her mother, was a philanderer all his life - and her mother knew about it. Watching two people fake a marriage has put her off the idea that true love exists and actually led to <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Self-harm" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">a bout of cutting</a> when she was younger. Working with animals, along with therapy, helped release her feelings in a more productive way, but her heart has some rather substantial walls around it and she's unwilling to risk it, even with all the feelings Zach stirs in her.<br><br><img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1329950867l/13144229.jpg" alt="" width="140" height="210" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><a href="http://www.amazon.com/Only-Have-Eyes-For-ebook/dp/B007BW34BM/ref=pd_sim_kstore_2?ie=UTF8&amp;m=AG56TWVU5XWC2" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> </a><br><br>Zach is a great tortured hero, simply because you don't realize how damaged he is at first glance. I loved him <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Only-Have-Eyes-For-ebook/dp/B007BW34BM/ref=pd_sim_kstore_2?ie=UTF8&amp;m=AG56TWVU5XWC2" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">in Sophie Sullivan's story</a>, when he beat the crap out of his best friend Jake for getting her pregnant, and he's always been a great brother and good businessman. But in this book we discover that Zach's strong resemblance to his father, who succumbed to a sudden aneurysm in his thirties leaving a wife and eight young children, has led Zach to avoid falling in love because he's not convinced that he'll be around for that long. The fast cars and faster women have been a natural outcome of this secret belief that his days are numbered, and he may not be able to let go of his pain to make a life with Heather.<br><br>Walk, don't run, to your nearest ebook vendor to purchase this book. Andre has once again crafted deep characters you instantly root for, praying they will work through their emotional baggage and realize the love of lifetime is at their fingertips if they would just take a chance. The dogs are incredible minor characters and seeing our favorite Sullivans (the ones already partnered happy and healthy and the ones still single having their clock ticking) gives you the feeling that you are catching up with friends.<br><br>I've put an Amazon alert so I'll be notified next time when Bella Andre publishes another book. I don't want to miss an hour of reading when Ryan Sullivan's book, <a href="http://www.bellaandre.com/comingsoon.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <em>Let Me Be the One</em>
</a>, comes out in the fall!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1222984426188405845" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3401630070" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3401630070" />
    <a title="MyMoonlightBird" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/99530684-mymoonlightbird"><img alt="MyMoonlightBird" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1562516155p2/99530684.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3401630070?book_show_action=true">Jun 20, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MyMoonlightBird" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MyMoonlightBird" href="/user/show/99530684-mymoonlightbird">MyMoonlightBird</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9789022575352" href="/book/show/26050444-als-je-van-mij-was">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3401630070" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6382248289464430826">* You do not need to read the previous entries to enjoy this book.<br/>** Book read in Dutch.<br/><br/>Zach Sullivan is a playboy and he is certain his wild ways will never change. But when his brother asks him to look after their terror puppy, he knows he needs some specialised help. Heather and her dog Atlas belong to the best dog trainers in the city, but this usually closed off woman might be unable to withstand the combined charismatic powers of Zach and the puppy. When they finally give in to their attra</span>
  <span id="freeText6382248289464430826" style="display:none">* You do not need to read the previous entries to enjoy this book.<br />** Book read in Dutch.<br /><br />Zach Sullivan is a playboy and he is certain his wild ways will never change. But when his brother asks him to look after their terror puppy, he knows he needs some specialised help. Heather and her dog Atlas belong to the best dog trainers in the city, but this usually closed off woman might be unable to withstand the combined charismatic powers of Zach and the puppy. When they finally give in to their attraction, all bets are off. But will they be able to make it work, because they're two very different people.<br /><br />Pro's:<br />+ The dogs in this story are great. Atlas is a loyal, quiet rescue Great Dane and Cuddles is a young, energetic Yorkie, but even though they are very different they just seem to be instant best friends. Cuddles's antics are great ( and any dogowners worst nightmare) and her instant connection to Zach is absolutly amazing.<br />+ Another well-told story that was very easy to read. Bella Andre always has a certain flow to her stories that make them very easy to get through and very entertaining. The characters in this book are total opposites and in the beginning, they don't even want to be involved with eachother. I really enjoy that angle and it never became obnoxious or boring. <br /><br />Con's:<br />- The description of how amazing and good-looking Zach is gets really boring, really quickly. After three times you'd think we'd know, but the author couldn't help herself in overpraising this characters abilities. For me, this really reduced my liking for this character and therefore I didn't enjoy this story as much as I could have.<br /><br />A very enjoyable read, I got a lot of entertainment out of this romance. The best thing for me were the dogs. I love dogs and if an author captures their personalities really well it scores big points on my entertainment meter. Zach was annoying, but overall I would really recommend this book. Heather is not too feminine, so if you like that type of heroine you might enjoy this book quite a lot. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6382248289464430826" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_341273762" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/341273762" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6915787-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/341273762?book_show_action=true">Jun 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/6915787-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer341273762" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10905816840974651913">Sexy, hotter then his movie star brother, filthy rich and with a puppy in tow – what women could resist the middle son, Zack, of the Sullivan’s Family? Well that is what he is wondering when he meets the equally sexy Heather Linsey and she promptly tells him she isn’t interested. <br/><br/>Zach will do anything for his family. So when Zack’s brother asks him to keep his puppy while his family is on vacation he can’t bring himself to say no - even though a puppy does not fit into his hectic life as the own</span>
  <span id="freeText10905816840974651913" style="display:none">Sexy, hotter then his movie star brother, filthy rich and with a puppy in tow – what women could resist the middle son, Zack, of the Sullivan’s Family? Well that is what he is wondering when he meets the equally sexy Heather Linsey and she promptly tells him she isn’t interested. <br /><br />Zach will do anything for his family. So when Zack’s brother asks him to keep his puppy while his family is on vacation he can’t bring himself to say no - even though a puppy does not fit into his hectic life as the owner of multiple car repair shops and busy bachelor. After just a few hours with “Cuddles”, the mischievous puppy, he is ready to pull his hair out. However, his life get’s even more complicated when a little old lady customer takes pity on him and sends Heather, a dog trainer, to him hoping she will take him on as a client and help train the little crazed puppy. <br /><br />From the moment Heather arrives at Zack’s service station the sparks begin to fly between them. And although Zack is charming and full of one-liners packed with sexual innuendo and comic relief Heather doesn’t want anything to do with him. She agrees to help him get started with puppy training but insists that he will work with another trainer long term and firmly draws a line. Little does she know that she is doing the one thing no one has ever done before – not falling for his charm or money and turning their attraction into a challenge. Zack is immediately hooked and the harder she tries to push him away – the harder he fights to get her. <br /><br />Heather has sworn off love – believing that it isn’t really real and just an act that her parents put on for her to cover the fact that her father has always been sleeping around. Zack’s charm sets her nerves on edge and it takes her really getting to know him before she see’s the man deep within. Luckily he is up for the challenge.<br /><br />Zack has no problem with love, in fact, he knows it’s wonderful which is why he has avoided it. Ever since Zack’s father died when he was just seven his biggest fear is that he will one day leave behind a widow to morn him. So he has kept women at a distance. And that was fine until he met Heather and subsequently now can’t imagine living a moment without her. But is enjoying whatever time he can have with her and possibly falling in love worth the risk of leaving her to a life without him if their time is cut short? It is a question he struggles with constantly. And can Heather learn that all men are not like her father?<br /><br /> Zack is a joy for both Heather and the reader to learn more about. They start off their relationship agreeing to keep things casual with no strings attached since that is all they both are comfortable with. But regardless of their concerns about developing things too emotionally, Zack is such a sweet guy that things can’t help but progress. He is funny and has a knack for making each simple moment they share into something memorable. If you have not read this series before this could be read as a stand-alone. However, most of the family (a total of eight siblings and his mom) makes appearances throughout and you will enjoy it more if you go back and read the previous books in the series. Although both characters have their own concerns about getting into something they both are mentally healthy and mature in their current lives. Their relationship progresses naturally and yet still at a relatively quick pace given their concerns. All in all though it is a believable story and masterfully written as all of Bella Andre’s books are. This one and the rest of this series should have their own space on the “to keep and read again and again” shelf!<br /><br />RATING: Five chocolate dipped strawberries enjoyed with a puppy in your lap!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10905816840974651913" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_377702907" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/377702907" />
    <a title="Jess" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1255781-jess"><img alt="Jess" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1502336592p2/1255781.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/377702907?book_show_action=true">Jul 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jess" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jess" href="/user/show/1255781-jess">Jess</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1255781-jess?shelf=family_sibling_series">family_sibling_series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1255781-jess?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer377702907" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17455646920331103180">Review posted: <a href='http://happilyeverafter-reads.blogspot.com/2012/09/review-if-you-were-mine-sullivans-5-by.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Happily Ever After - Reads</a><br/><br/>In a family of overachievers, Zach almost blends into the background a bit. A huge success in his own right, owning a chain of highly successful auto repair shops, he’s never been in nor wanted a long term relationship. Having a father, who he resembles completely, die suddenly at a young age, Zach is convinced that he’ll have the same thing happen to him. So he lives life fully, but will never let anyone get too close out of fear that he’ll leave them al</span>
  <span id="freeText17455646920331103180" style="display:none">Review posted: <a href="http://happilyeverafter-reads.blogspot.com/2012/09/review-if-you-were-mine-sullivans-5-by.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Happily Ever After - Reads</a><br /><br />In a family of overachievers, Zach almost blends into the background a bit. A huge success in his own right, owning a chain of highly successful auto repair shops, he’s never been in nor wanted a long term relationship. Having a father, who he resembles completely, die suddenly at a young age, Zach is convinced that he’ll have the same thing happen to him. So he lives life fully, but will never let anyone get too close out of fear that he’ll leave them alone like his father did to his mother and his siblings.<br /><br />Heather owns a dog training/doggie day care company and when she comes across Zach struggling to take care of a puppy he was tasked with dog sitting for two weeks. Heather steps in and demands he put himself and his little puppy into training. Zach does because he wants to be around Heather as much as possible, but while he starts bonding with the troublesome pup, he also starts bonding with Heather. He doesn’t want a future with her, his fear of dying young dictates pretty much everything in his life, so the couple decides that sex-only is the way to go.<br /><br />I enjoyed Zach and Heather. I loved the addition of the dogs, sometimes the little extras like pets and kids that are thrown into a romance can take away from the main characters, but in this case, I found the pups charming and they added to the overall story. The relationship between Heather and Zach is simply hot. They go into it for sex only, very steamy sex, and once Zach’s family, namely his nosy sisters find out about Heather, they want her in the family permanently.<br /><br />The pace of their relationship was nice, they slowly become attached to each other, but Zach has a hard time fully committing. I really like that Heather came clean with him about her past, she put all her insecurities out there for Zach to know about including her dysfunctional family and how she dealt with her father’s betrayal as a teen. Zach needed a good smack for not trusting Heather with his own fears of following in his father’s footsteps and believing that he’s destined to die too young. I was frustrated at him toward the end for creating angst that didn’t need to happen. But that’s my only issue in an otherwise sweet love story.<br /><br />I also enjoyed seeing the other Sullivan siblings that have already found love show up and get little updates on them. There’s a birth in this story (finally!) and seeing all the siblings fall in love with a new little Sullivan is very sweet and even more so seeing this new love through Zach’s eyes.<br /><br />I continue to be enchanted by this series. The siblings are all so likeable, even in their perfect, overachieving lives. But it works because they’re a close knit family, full of love and they’re simply nice characters to follow and want happy endings for. </span>
  <a data-text-id="17455646920331103180" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_711525391" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/711525391" />
    <a title="Autum (Escape between the Covers)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498526-autum-escape-between-the-covers"><img alt="Autum (Escape between the Covers)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515109213p2/5498526.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/711525391?book_show_action=true">Sep 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Autum (Escape between the Covers)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Autum (Escape between the Covers)" href="/user/show/5498526-autum-escape-between-the-covers">Autum (Escape between the Covers)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer711525391" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2349062080886532603">I have to say that I have come to love the Sullivans thanks to Bella Andre. I want to read about all of them over and over. Zach is the middle son of the Sullivans and is the one he himself feels is the most likely to end up like his dad. It seems that the family does not know he feels this way; except maybe his mother. He is asked to take care of his soon to be nieces dog. A friend thinks he needs some help and enlists Heather. Zach has some issues as he has decided to not get in a committed re</span>
  <span id="freeText2349062080886532603" style="display:none">I have to say that I have come to love the Sullivans thanks to Bella Andre. I want to read about all of them over and over. Zach is the middle son of the Sullivans and is the one he himself feels is the most likely to end up like his dad. It seems that the family does not know he feels this way; except maybe his mother. He is asked to take care of his soon to be nieces dog. A friend thinks he needs some help and enlists Heather. Zach has some issues as he has decided to not get in a committed relationship whether with a woman or even a poor little puppy. But Heather comes to help out with the puppy and then Zach decides he wants to know her more. Heather has decided long ago a relationship is not for her. Not after seeing how her father treated and still treats her mother. The lies her father told her and the fact that her mother, pretends everything is perfect. Well it was just too much for the young Heather and she became a cutter. She over came that terrible time but she is guarded about relationships. Even though she is attracted to Zach a lot more than she wants to admit. Though it does not take the two long to hook up, and start saying I love you. They both had to over come their personal horrors/issues. I think Bella wrote this very well and I loved how she shows us how they both leaned on each other. To help with the others sorrows and problems, and what is even more romantic is that they learned to accept the other as they were flaws and all.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2349062080886532603" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I have enjoyed every one of these Sullivan books to date and this one was no different.<br /><br /><br />Heather has never given love a chance. Having grown up in a family where love was just an illusion, she had her view of love shattered at a young age.<br /><br /><br />Zach is a lady's man. Rich and Good looking, he never has problems finding willing women to share his bed with no strings attached.<br /><br /><br />Upon his first meeting with Heather, Zach knows there is something different about her. Zach must prove to him they are nothing like his parents.<br /><br /><br />I loved the subtle changes in Zach. I felt like his fall into love was a smooth and steady one. He was not afraid to let his feelings be known once he had them. The chemistry between him and Heather was great. This is one of those book couples you route for the whole time. I had tears in my eyes at points. I loved that Zach's story gave us more insight into Jack Sullivan.<br /><br /><br />The added bonus of reading about the dogs, Cuddles and Atlas, was great. I loved their relationship with each other it sounded like one of those email strings of pictures with odd "best friends" in the animal world. Too cute!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1017500036" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1653409568040476774">Bella Andre says "my favourite romances have always been about families. I love following brothers and sisters and cousins from book to book" and I agree, many of my favourite easy read romances follow this theme. Bella Andre, in my opinion, has a similar style to Bernadette Marie and Melody Anne, and focuses on the Sullivan family from San Francisco. What makes series romances like this successful for me is the interaction between the brothers and sisters, the teasing and ribbing.<br/><br/>Book 5 is abou</span>
  <span id="freeText1653409568040476774" style="display:none">Bella Andre says "my favourite romances have always been about families. I love following brothers and sisters and cousins from book to book" and I agree, many of my favourite easy read romances follow this theme. Bella Andre, in my opinion, has a similar style to Bernadette Marie and Melody Anne, and focuses on the Sullivan family from San Francisco. What makes series romances like this successful for me is the interaction between the brothers and sisters, the teasing and ribbing.<br /><br />Book 5 is about Zach Sullivan and Heather Linsey. Zach is lumbered with his niece's puppy Cuddles for 2 weeks and he's running around in circles after it. Heather is a dog trainer and steps in to help train Cuddles. Both of them have strong ideas about lasting relationships. Heather is scarred by the memory of her parent's marriage and Zach sees his similarities with his dad and worries he will suffer the same fate.<br /><br />It sounds a bit odd and quaint but the doggy friendship between Atlas and Cuddles was very cute and fun. Zach is a charmer without being smarmy and Heather is strong willed and plucky. <br /><br />The series is getting a bit samey, the characters are different and the story of how they get together varies but the rest is fairly similar between the books, including the rather dry sex scenes.</span>

  <span id="freeText14028298906724910208" style="display:none"><b> December 2016 Review: </b><br /><br />This was an incredible read. I love the Sullivans series. He is a mechanic in his shop as well. He used to be a player trying to get any girl's attention. Then Heather came along and changed that. Can't wait to read Ryan and Vicki's story in Let Me Be The One! Overall, an amazing read.</span>

  <span id="freeText16009349994689652291" style="display:none">This series keeps getting better and better. This book was one of the most intense because both were fighting love with such intensity that it snuck up on both of them. Zach made a bet with his sister Lori on the day of his sister Sophie and best friend Jake's wedding on who would be the next to fall in love. Zach was confident that he would never fall in love until he met Heather his new dog trainer and her beauty struck him to the core. Heather does not believe in love because of her father and Zach is not looking for love because of his father. She does not trust men because her father constantly cheated on her mother. While Zach who is very similar to his father believes he will die young like him and does not want to eave someone the way his father left his mother. They are wonderful together and there dogs Atlas (her's) and Cuddles (his) are just as in love as they are. I can't wait for Ryan and Vicki's story because Zach told him he was next. <span id="freeTextContainer9027575661959614527">Another easy, fast read. I tell you, if you're ever on the look out for something to escape in, there's no better distraction than the Sullivans - the men, specifically.<br/><br/>This book is about Zach, love em and leave em kind of guy, whose expertise in cars equal his expertise in flirtation and seduction. But he may have his hands full with a puppy and the dog trainer who won't give him the time of day. When Heather acquiesced to a sex only relationship with Zach, she didn't anticipate the ease with w</span>
  <span id="freeText9027575661959614527" style="display:none">Another easy, fast read. I tell you, if you're ever on the look out for something to escape in, there's no better distraction than the Sullivans - the men, specifically.<br /><br />This book is about Zach, love em and leave em kind of guy, whose expertise in cars equal his expertise in flirtation and seduction. But he may have his hands full with a puppy and the dog trainer who won't give him the time of day. When Heather acquiesced to a sex only relationship with Zach, she didn't anticipate the ease with which the man could get under her skin. Having been a witness to just how much it would hurt for a loved one to betray her trust, she wasn't too keen to letting anybody in. But Zach is also a go-getter, never-give-up type of guy, so even if Heather freezes him out, he's got the moves to thaw her out. Besides, who wouldn't want that kind of arrangement?<br /><br />So these two has issues that could've added another layer to their story. But I guess Ms. Andre decided not to explore it too much because it would add a pinch of angst to an otherwise, smooth-sailing, safe series.<br /><br />If You Were Mine is enjoyable enough; but don't expect more than what the summary's given.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9027575661959614527" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer734111639" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer4615276840904505616">If You Were Mine by Bella Andre is a delightful addition to the Sullivan series. Zach and Heather meet when Zach is dog watching for his niece while she’s away on vacation. Their antics and interactions as well as those of their dogs makes for a charming and entertaining read. Both Zach and Heather are instantly attracted and Zach is determined to win Heather over while she is just as determined to keep her distance. Though they do agree on one thing, neither one is looking for love. Their love </span>
  <span id="freeText4615276840904505616" style="display:none">If You Were Mine by Bella Andre is a delightful addition to the Sullivan series. Zach and Heather meet when Zach is dog watching for his niece while she’s away on vacation. Their antics and interactions as well as those of their dogs makes for a charming and entertaining read. Both Zach and Heather are instantly attracted and Zach is determined to win Heather over while she is just as determined to keep her distance. Though they do agree on one thing, neither one is looking for love. Their love story is all about finding just what you need to make yourself and your life whole.<br /><br />If You Were Mine is a well written, fast paced love story. The characters are likeable and well-drawn. There are tender moments and sexy ones, moments of laughter and glimpses of heartache. It all combines together into a story that is a pleasure to read. If You Were Mine and the entire Sullivan series is recommended for fans of contemporary romance.<br /></span>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('HW4tplRwPEr8PY33yjHFRuw7G0WUPTLRinRhYuVlFPmgUiRvvbhynjjnZffKZvvCzMf2uQ9eRMR7dWChFKcKSA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('jUMSRmppBFfKvrpL/LT1hAnMtXUrL8i+0EgvxUD3368wfxuPg6FKgw5kUkv848sAKTBYibBMvqshSS4GsTXBHg==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer16338416385587184679">Bella Andre is the New York Times, USA Today and Publishers Weekly bestselling author of “The Sullivans” and “The Morrisons” series.<br/><br/>Having sold more than 9 million books, Bella Andre’s novels have been #1 bestsellers around the world and have appeared on the New York Times and USA Today bestseller lists 84 times. She has been the #1 Ranked Author at Amazon (on a top 10 list that included Nora Robe</span>
  <span id="freeText16338416385587184679" style="display:none">Bella Andre is the New York Times, USA Today and Publishers Weekly bestselling author of “The Sullivans” and “The Morrisons” series.<br /><br />Having sold more than 9 million books, Bella Andre’s novels have been #1 bestsellers around the world and have appeared on the New York Times and USA Today bestseller lists 84 times. She has been the #1 Ranked Author at Amazon (on a top 10 list that included Nora Roberts, JK Rowling, James Patterson and Steven King). Apple iBooks named her one of the "bestselling authors of all time." And Publishers Weekly named Oak Press (the publishing company she created to publish her own books) the Fastest-Growing Independent Publisher in the US. After signing a groundbreaking 7-figure print-only deal with Harlequin MIRA, Bella’s “The Sullivans” series is being released in paperback in the US, Canada, and Australia.<br /><br />Known for “sensual, empowered stories enveloped in heady romance” (Publishers Weekly), her books have been Cosmopolitan Magazine “Red Hot Reads” twice and have been translated into ten languages. Winner of the Award of Excellence, The Washington Post called her “One of the top writers in America” and she has been featured by Entertainment Weekly, NPR, USA Today, Forbes, The Wall Street Journal, and TIME Magazine. A graduate of Stanford University, she has given keynote speeches at publishing conferences from Copenhagen to Berlin to San Francisco, including a standing-room-only keynote at Book Expo America in New York City.<br /><br />Bella also writes the New York Times bestselling Four Weddings and a Fiasco series as Lucy Kevin. Her “sweet” contemporary romances also include the new Walker Island series written as Lucy Kevin.<br /><br />If not behind her computer, you can find her reading her favorite authors, hiking, swimming or laughing. Married with two children, Bella splits her time between the Northern California wine country, a 100 year old log cabin in the Adirondacks, and a flat in London overlooking the Thames..<br /><br />* * * * * * *<br /><br />For digital/eBook, audiobook, foreign licensing, conference keynote and press inquiries, please contact Bella at bella@bellaandre.com</span>
